## 20. Phase 18 - Wait For Store Acceptance

`2026-04-28T21:41:17.371301Z -> 2026-04-28T21:41:28.627207Z` - `7` events

### Screen
Waiting for store acceptance

### User Action
User waits while the store/backend decides what happens next.

### What happened
The app listens for WebSocket updates and mirrors order status in checkout state.

### Bloc
`CheckoutBloc`

### Events
```text

nav MaterialPageRoute<void> -> MaterialPageRoute<dynamic>
```

## 21. Phase 19 - Payment / Free Order Handling

`2026-04-28T21:41:20.350896Z -> 2026-04-28T21:42:15.729812Z` - `11` events

### Screen
Checkout payment step

### User Action
The app completes payment or free-order handling.

### What happened
Payment APIs or free-order APIs decide whether the order can continue.

### Bloc
`CheckoutBloc`, `AllCartsBloc`, `OrderDetailsBloc`

### Events
```text
CheckoutBloc.PlaceFreeOrder (last payload: PlaceFreeOrder())
AllCartsBloc.ClearCart (last payload: ClearCart(1))
nav MaterialPageRoute<dynamic> -> MaterialPageRoute<void>
```

### API Request - Mark free order paid
```http
POST https://lastmile.fainzy.tech/v1/core/order/free/
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "amount": 0.0,
  "order_id": "#482976",
  "currency": "jpy",
  "subentity_id": 1,
  "coupon": 294
}
```

## Issues & Possible Solutions

### 1. OTP echoed in API response

**Evidence**: `https://lastmile.fainzy.tech/v1/auth/otp/send/` returned `data=7497`.

**Likely root cause**: The backend exposes the OTP in the response body.

**Possible solution**: Only echo OTP in local/debug environments and mask OTP fields in production logs.

### 2. HTML error page returned from API

**Evidence**: `POST https://fainzy.tech/v1/core/possible-location/` returned HTTP `404` with an HTML body.

**Likely root cause**: The backend returned a framework error page instead of a structured JSON API error.

**Possible solution**: Return JSON errors from the backend and have the client log only a short HTML preview.

### 3. GET request returned HTTP 201

**Evidence**: `GET https://lastmile.fainzy.tech/v1/core/orders/?user=27` returned `201`.

**Likely root cause**: The server is using a creation status for a read operation.

**Possible solution**: Return `200` for reads; keep the client tolerant of the 2xx family while the backend is fixed.

### 4. Empty image URL reached cache manager

**Evidence**: `2026-04-28T21:40:40.878350Z` captured `No host specified in URI`.

**Likely root cause**: A widget attempted to load an empty string as a network image URL.

**Possible solution**: Guard image URLs with `Uri.tryParse(url)?.hasAbsolutePath`/`hasScheme` and render a fallback image.

### 5. Large metadata object is posted back to backend

**Evidence**: `POST https://lastmile.fainzy.tech/v1/core/orders/` sends nested restaurant/subentity metadata.

**Likely root cause**: The client posts server-owned metadata instead of stable identifiers.

**Possible solution**: Send IDs and user-entered fields only; let the backend hydrate restaurant/order metadata.

### 6. Binary PDF body logged inline

**Evidence**: `GET https://lastmile.fainzy.tech/v1/core/generate-receipt/544/` logged a binary-like response body.

**Likely root cause**: The logger does not detect PDF/binary content before serialising the body.

**Possible solution**: Log `{contentType, byteLength, fileName}` for binary responses instead of the body.

### 7. OrderDetailsBloc closes an uninitialized subscription

**Evidence**: `2026-04-28T21:44:05.406227Z` captured `LateInitializationError: Field '_streamSubscription@222435990' has not been initialized.`.

**Likely root cause**: `late StreamSubscription` is cancelled in `close()` even when it was never assigned.

**Possible solution**: Make the subscription nullable and cancel with `await _streamSubscription?.cancel()`.

### 8. Socket lifecycle churn

**Evidence**: `14` socket lifecycle events were captured.

**Likely root cause**: The socket is started/stopped repeatedly as auth and navigation state changes.

**Possible solution**: Key the socket singleton by user id and reconnect only when that key changes.
